<script id="delphi-bubble-script">
window.delphi = {...(window.delphi ?? {}) };
window.delphi.bubble = {
config: "72223e25-fc63-4d74-b027-91f40f6b9c14",

},

// Add global function to close/open Delphi that can be called from other components
window.toggleDelphiWidget = function(shouldOpen) {
// Wait until Delphi is fully loaded
if (!window.delphi || !window.delphi.frame) {
console.log('[DelphiEmbed] Cannot toggle: widget not fully initialized');
return false;
}

try {
// Get the trigger button - use multiple selectors to be safe
const delphiTrigger = document.querySelector('#delphi-bubble-trigger') ||
document.querySelector('.delphi-injected[role="button"]') ||
document.querySelector('.delphi-bubble-button');

if (!delphiTrigger) {
console.log('[DelphiEmbed] Cannot toggle: trigger button not found');
return false;
}

// Check current state - also use attribute data-is-open as backup
const isCurrentlyOpen = !!document.querySelector('.delphi-bubble-open') ||
delphiTrigger.getAttribute('data-is-open') === 'true';

// If shouldOpen is undefined, toggle. Otherwise respect the parameter
const shouldToggle = (shouldOpen === undefined) ? true : (shouldOpen !== isCurrentlyOpen);

if (shouldToggle) {
console.log(`[DelphiEmbed] ${isCurrentlyOpen ? 'Closing' : 'Opening'} Delphi widget`);
delphiTrigger.click();
return true;
}

return false;
} catch (error) {
console.error('[DelphiEmbed] Error toggling widget:', error);
return false;
}
};

// Function to close Delphi if it's open
window.closeDelphiWidget = function() {
return window.toggleDelphiWidget(false);
};

window.hideDelphiWidget = function() {
window.closeDelphiWidget()
const container = document.getElementById('delphi-root-encapsulation')
if (container) container.style.display = 'none'
}

window.showDelphiWidget = function() {
const container = document.getElementById('delphi-root-encapsulation')
if (container) container.style.display = 'block'
}

window.delphi.coachEnabled = null;

window.addEventListener('turbo:load', () => {
if (!window.delphi || !window.delphi.frame) return

// Check if Omni panel is expanded via data attribute
const isOmniExpanded = document.body.dataset.omniPanelExpanded === 'true'

// Hide widget if editor is open OR if coach is not enabled OR if Omni is open
if (window.location.pathname.includes('editor') ||
window.location.pathname.includes('workflow_steps') ||
isOmniExpanded) {
window.hideDelphiWidget()
} else if (window.delphi.coachEnabled) {
window.showDelphiWidget()
}
})
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
// Store the SSO token for authentication
window.delphi.auth = {
token: "eyJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiJ9.eyJlbWFpbCI6ImFsZXhzdWRha292QHByb2RpZ3kubmV0IiwiZXhwIjoxNzY1NTEzMDIzfQ.a0KNhFbXFb6esCJS5d7CSG1WgASK-gJnCmEQ13XPE0tiI6yp2L5Xu96mHBK_HtPy3rvnzfDg0ATxWcjNmagHnh6D9qKH-v9RK8Vv0h0pMz4Tlk-7dWdkfiiSkytaUHnPNq325QtXpcSWU9Kwzr3MCTPc_LqvVHrvi4FSmJxBwPAMtEvKvja7yoxx_b_qJAvNi2UFLWBvri8V6osb9bQvR2zJywlTpYEWIg9RpgHMRW96TralNAmSGhwHVo0D0NpdW5Zj7lQ-MPR3F_ghAXE09H9mMOGcbNYwBKaDZuYU8U0GcvxXOtHTEMEzvYYI8IxXi4T2frN5YtfuAKt9FeKzAw"
};

// Define a robust class for handling Delphi embed authentication
if (!window.DelphiEmbed) {
window.DelphiEmbed = class {
constructor(token) {
this.token = token;
this.maxRetries = 10;
this.retryDelay = 1000;
this.loadTimeout = 20000;
this.retryCount = 0;
this.initialized = false;
this.authAttempted = false;
// IMPORTANT: Delphi's actual domain is different depending on environment
// We'll detect it dynamically rather than hard-coding
this.possibleOrigins = [
"https://embed.delphi.ai",
"https://funnels.starters.io",
"https://chat.delphi.ai",
"*" // Fallback
];
}
async initialize() {
// Add a safety check in case we're already initialized
if (this.initialized) {
console.log('[DelphiEmbed] Already initialized, skipping initialization');
return;
}
// Set up a global event listener for postMessage events from Delphi or its proxies
window.addEventListener('message', (event) => {
// Check if the message is from a known Delphi domain or relevant to Delphi
const isDelphiRelated = event.origin.includes('delphi.ai') ||
event.origin.includes('funnels.starters.io') ||
(event.data && event.data.type &&
event.data.type.toString().includes('delphi') ||
event.data.type === 'sso_login' ||
event.data.type === 'sso_request' ||
event.data.type === 'ready');
if (isDelphiRelated) {
// Store the actual origin for future communication
this.lastKnownOrigin = event.origin;
// If we receive a ready event or auth request, try to authenticate
if (event.data && (
event.data.type === 'delphi_frame_ready' ||
event.data.type === 'sso_request' ||
event.data.type === 'ready'
)) {
this.authenticateEmbed(event.source, event.origin);
}
// If we receive a auth success event, mark as initialized
if (event.data && event.data.type === 'sso_success') {
console.log('[DelphiEmbed] Authentication successful');
this.initialized = true;
clearInterval(this.retryInterval);
}
// If we receive an auth error, log it
if (event.data && event.data.type === 'sso_error') {
console.error('[DelphiEmbed] Authentication error:', event.data);
// Attempt one more authentication after a short delay
if (!this.authRetryAttempted) {
this.authRetryAttempted = true;
setTimeout(() => this.findAndAuthenticate(), 2000);
}
}
}
});
// Wait for a bit longer to ensure the frame is ready
setTimeout(() => this.findAndAuthenticate(), 2000);
}
findAndAuthenticate() {
// Check for the frame using multiple methods
if (this.checkDelphiFrame()) {
return;
}
// Start the retry mechanism if we didn't find the frame
this.startRetryMechanism();
}
checkDelphiFrame() {
// Try different methods to find the Delphi iframe
const frames = [
window.delphi?.frame,
document.querySelector('iframe[id^="delphi"]'),
document.querySelector('iframe[src*="delphi.ai"]'),
document.querySelector('iframe[src*="starters.io"]'),
document.querySelector('iframe[class*="delphi"]'),
// Get all iframes and find one that might be Delphi
...Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('iframe')).filter(f =>
(f.src && (
f.src.includes('delphi.ai') ||
f.src.includes('starters.io')
)) ||
f.id?.includes('delphi') ||
f.className?.includes('delphi')
)
].filter(Boolean);
// Use the first frame found
const frame = frames[0];
if (frame) {
window.delphi.frame = frame; // Store reference

// Hide widget if editor is open
if (window.location.pathname.includes('editor') || window.location.pathname.includes('workflow_steps')) {
window.hideDelphiWidget()
}
// Detect the actual origin from the iframe's src
let targetOrigin = "*"; // Default fallback
try {
if (frame.src) {
const url = new URL(frame.src);
targetOrigin = url.origin;
// Store for future use
this.lastKnownOrigin = targetOrigin;
}
} catch (error) {
console.warn('[DelphiEmbed] Could not determine frame origin, using wildcard (*)', error);
}
// Try to authenticate with this frame using the detected origin
this.authenticateEmbed(frame.contentWindow, targetOrigin);
return true;
}
return false;
}
startRetryMechanism() {
// Clear any existing interval
if (this.retryInterval) {
clearInterval(this.retryInterval);
}
// Set up a retry mechanism
this.retryInterval = setInterval(() => {
if (this.initialized) {
clearInterval(this.retryInterval);
return;
}
if (this.checkDelphiFrame()) {
// We found the frame, authentication attempted
// Keep the interval running to check for success
this.retryCount++;
} else {
this.retryCount++;
}
if (this.retryCount >= this.maxRetries) {
console.warn('[DelphiEmbed] Max retries reached, failed to complete authentication');
clearInterval(this.retryInterval);
}
}, this.retryDelay);
// Set a timeout to eventually give up
setTimeout(() => {
if (this.retryInterval) {
console.warn('[DelphiEmbed] Timed out waiting for authentication to complete');
clearInterval(this.retryInterval);
}
}, this.loadTimeout);
}
authenticateEmbed(target = null, origin = null) {
// Avoid duplicate auth attempts in quick succession
if (this.authAttempted && Date.now() - this.lastAuthAttempt < 2000) {
return;
}
this.authAttempted = true;
this.lastAuthAttempt = Date.now();
// Find the Delphi iframe if not provided
const frame = target || window.delphi?.frame ||
document.querySelector('iframe[id^="delphi"]') ||
document.querySelector('iframe[src*="delphi.ai"]') ||
document.querySelector('iframe[src*="starters.io"]');
// Use the provided origin, last known origin, or detect from frame
let targetOrigin = origin || this.lastKnownOrigin || "*";
// If we have a frame and no specific origin, try to get it from the frame
if (frame?.src && !origin && !this.lastKnownOrigin) {
try {
targetOrigin = new URL(frame.src).origin;
} catch (e) {
console.warn('[DelphiEmbed] Error determining origin from frame:', e);
}
}
if (!frame && !target) {
return;
}
try {
// Create a message object with the token
const message = {
type: "sso_login",
token: this.token
};
// Use postMessage to send the token
if (target && typeof target.postMessage === 'function') {
// Try with specific origin first
try {
target.postMessage(message, targetOrigin);
} catch (e) {
// If that fails, try with wildcard
target.postMessage(message, "*");
}
} else if (frame?.contentWindow) {
// Try with specific origin first
try {
frame.contentWindow.postMessage(message, targetOrigin);
} catch (e) {
// If that fails, try with wildcard
frame.contentWindow.postMessage(message, "*");
}
} else {
// Last resort fallback
window.postMessage(message, "*");
}
} catch (error) {
console.error('[DelphiEmbed] Error sending SSO token:', error);
}
}
};
}

// Initialize the SSO authentication
window.initializeDelphiSSO = function() {
// Check if we already have an instance
if (window.delphiSSO) {
console.log('[DelphiEmbed] Instance already exists, re-initializing');
}

window.delphiSSO = new window.DelphiEmbed(window.delphi.auth.token);
window.delphiSSO.initialize().catch(error => {
console.error('[DelphiEmbed] Initialization error:', error);
});
}

// Wait for DOM to be ready
if (document.readyState === 'complete' || document.readyState === 'interactive') {
setTimeout(initializeDelphiSSO, 1000);
} else {
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
setTimeout(initializeDelphiSSO, 1000);
});
}
</script>

// Intercept mixpanel track calls to rename CommandBar events
const originalTrack = mixpanel.track;
mixpanel.track = function(eventName, properties) {
if (eventName.startsWith('CommandBar ')) {
// Remove "CommandBar " prefix and format the remaining text
// "CommandBar help_hub_opened" -> "Help Hub Opened"
eventName = eventName
.replace('CommandBar ', '')
.split('_')
.map(word => word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.slice(1))
.join(' ');
}
// Call original track with renamed event
originalTrack.call(this, eventName, properties);
};

function openChatWidgetOnLoad() {
// Check if fdchat=true is in the URL parameters
const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const shouldOpenChat = urlParams.get('fdchat') === 'true';
// Get chat closed status from local storage (defaults to false if not found)
const chatManuallyClosed = localStorage.getItem('freshchat_manually_closed') === 'true';
// Clear the manually closed flag if fdchat=true is specified
if (shouldOpenChat && chatManuallyClosed) {
localStorage.removeItem('freshchat_manually_closed');
}
// Open the chat if:
// 1. fdchat=true is in the URL, OR
// 2. User has an active chat AND hasn't manually closed the chat
if (shouldOpenChat || ("710467" && "false" === "true" && !chatManuallyClosed)) {
if (window.fcWidget.isOpen() != true) {
window.fcWidget.open();
}
}
}

window.fcWidget.on("widget:opened", function() {
setChatStatusOnUser(true);
// Reset the manually closed flag when opened
localStorage.removeItem('freshchat_manually_closed');
});
window.fcWidget.on("widget:closed", function() {
setChatStatusOnUser(false);
// Set a flag in localStorage to remember user manually closed the chat
localStorage.setItem('freshchat_manually_closed', 'true');

fetch(window.location.origin + "/account/set_user_chat_status", {

'Content-Type': 'application/json',

})

});
});
